The idea was simply to celebrate summer and translate that to a greeting card to send to friends and clients. The result is simple, smart, elegant and plain beautiful.</p>\n\n<p><q class=\"pullquote\">A blue striped curtain represents for us the essence of that retro chic summer.</q></p>\n\n<div class=\"imgsGrid\"><img src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/gb7dJ27ziuh_V_8C_46QkThvp0mHKJTg6IKvsEwRlpPA14XvEAxdML2le5QNZgw2de-po-NK-tX0YsRBZyLewuIKvmCmWBpMDOWgmIRLU7eO8ZDu22ygVKLsrGm0VKfU-7yAN9bF\" /><img src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/vU91Afu60Q2_EW5U4vZSJ_xBeJLX0gTOxfcADa0dXQAhm6KldnxIo6V8QMTStpP_AyuZMJpqAAoA-qlYmy3uuJED0U05ERzBfD0_75JmImcPD_3QlhVMUKc9WEGeWbOsjGftw8Cz\" /><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/dCKRJUhTswrZaXCsouwCaZFcWAao1AYOLE8gwWggz9bbPIB25x7rQ0wTf8ssCACV2xO_QsuP665sI19MNuELoR_a60sb52JzfObwq9rFQjDkrl6U1tD-EevXcGyXNN9-tR-W8KpH\" /><img src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/fVjT4LAiLueN646BUBi2nw9SD4jQF7wzJvz6x6we_jTw5mpsKw54DW05D7cmNtWqP4K0O0JVZ1IpIFAlv5B3NOnU3zddsGgZadZFoJ7mMChhPaYW8CogoLljHlbdKcj-f1K3y7N0\" /><img src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/HyFZFJM4EN36rf0OE5OTT1yPEqU2IZaOdCd-rjqGbpNMb1EGBecNDCJC1M-m27V_Zi205Ht_KON6jjalIvb2GRAiFJ1gYMs9x9tKmdBNd4eJDOMlQy9x3ZLn3cJsWFW5Ql8_4-w_\" /><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/QJ9lips7SfM4g2siSu0hStcdg2uaQ7aXIbrl7OuZFwtdpEWlflsOSDDAfzkqmpkYCgHpaUoJfKfZFWiEb2lRGRZxqJZE4a0rT10nT1nsbGHaJyJs8KxWTCSMcZQUTz49x0hE5_Le\" /></div>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>We love summer!⁠ It was the perfect excuse to send a greeting card to some of our friends, clients and collaborators. ⁠We wanted to thank them for their support and interest in our new, personal and exciting adventure, and also to celebrate the six months of our studio.⁠ We also love to play and experiment with stripes and lines! A blue striped curtain represents for us the essence of that retro chic summer. ⁠It is a classic pattern found in many objects and images representing the perfect relaxing summer: sun beds, beach towels and umbrellas, cabins and many other iconic items.⁠ Let’s enjoy the Summer Breeze!⁠⠀</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<h3>Motion Design</h3>\n\n<div data-oembed-url=\"https://vimeo.com/352332319\">\n<div href=\"https://www.behance.net/Shangning\">Shangning Wang</a> shared a personal project/ concept project/ student thesis project for the branding for COP 25 UN Climate Change Conference. <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/Shangning\">Shangning</a> discloses that this is not the official branding design of the event. This one was not selected by the event. This was only designed for education and communication purposes (designed in 2016). This project has no affiliation with UN COP's brand. For us it really doesn’t matter as our focus is on the translation of idea to a design recommendation, and personally speaking, the designer really nailed it. </p>\n\n<h3>Logo + Identity</h3>\n\n<div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/andrewpopplestone\">Andrew Popplestone</a> shared an awesome motion design case study for the Sky Sports rebrand. As part of the successful Sky Sports rebrand, Sky Creative Advertising tapped <a href=\"https://territorystudio.com/\">Territory</a> to design new opening titles and content for the dedicated Super League channel. </p>\n\n<p>With a vision to celebrate Sky's coverage of the sport with fresh energy, the brief included a 45 second opening title sequence for Sky Sports Super League, a 20 second generic Rugby League sequence and multiple bumpers. Designed to tie in with Sky Sports rebranding and its emphasis on personality, Territory was asked to push beyond genre conventions with a modern twist on the spirit of the game. The result is a highly stylised 2D cel animation that features a dynamic collage of all the Super League team mascots. Created to tell the story of the battle for the championship, the title sequence conveys the energy, drama and passion of the sport.</p>\n\n<div data-oembed-url=\"https://player.vimeo.com/video/342257876\">\n<div style=\"max-width:1620px;margin:auto;\">\n<div style=\"left: 0; width: 100%; height: 0; position: relative; padding-bottom: Firm, Page — Case Study\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/handsome-new-foundation-global-architecture-firm-page-case-study\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_page.png\" width=\"1900\" height=\"1534\" alt=\"Handsome New Foundation for Global Architecture Firm, Page — Case Study\" title=\"Handsome New Foundation for Global Architecture Firm, Page — Case Study\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>04.06.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>The amazing team over at <a href=\"https://handsome.is/case-study/page/\">handsome</a> shared a case study of the new web design for <a href=\"https://www.pagethink.com/\">Page</a>, a global multidisciplinary architecture and engineering firm, has partnered with branding and experience design agency handsome to evolve their brand for the digital age and redesign their website into an experience that was worthy of their talent, expertise, and passion for their work.</p>\n\n<p>After 100+ years of award-winning work and expansion to cities around the globe, Page’s website had become a tangled ecosystem built over many years by many administrators. It failed to serve their clients, potential hires, and even their own team. From the content quagmire of global offices, teams, and editors, the handsome team synthesized these many voices into coherent and structured content pillars.</p>\n\n<p>They united the Page team around the following: </p>\n\n<ul><li aria-level=\"1\">Design that makes lives better.</li>\n\t<li aria-level=\"1\">Creativity. Collaboration. Commitment.</li>\n\t<li aria-level=\"1\">One Firm. One Voice.</li>\n\t<li aria-level=\"1\">Always forward. People first.</li>\n</ul><p><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/QrGxXosJTEkt_eh3kJ6LJ5tvaVX5s65NvcSlDkLzA61P0AZIX4hI7figXKl3RZQj_yu3uUuPQAPpfR4lfheKM3Sc7Qkz0H5GQICGoCOaeJ7OLom0aJIpaGo2a31mC05ryuEPApsa\" /></p>\n\n<h3>From Templates to Modules</h3>\n\n<p>In addition, the previous platform relied on templates with nearly no flexibility for new content types and storytelling. Rather than simply refresh existing templates, our design team constructed a modular design system. This system of content blocks allows novice users the structure to easily create pages that look great and advanced users the flexibility to break expectations and invent differentiated page types.</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>Our development team worked hand-in-glove with our designers to ensure that our beautiful front-end experience was matched by an equally elegant CMS.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p>Today, Page is unified around an online brand and website experience that truly matches their ambitions. We managed to marry an seamless customer interface with robust tools for the teams that create these experiences.</p>\n\n<div class=\"imgsGrid\"><img src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/DnjzAMRh9M5xu-fZL7WbElCFeF4zgwQK7yuDx3AkECZYvH-br_1XdNQlTJsgl9nHshnFrYt7H-JiBdk29LbZhZHR1ff8JFplIliylnkv4TU3oMzgKBAUpL7JpzG6WMVpuTKcINfR\" /><img
